		| sed -e '$s/\\$//') > BLD-POTFILES-t \
	    && chmod a-w BLD-POTFILES-t \
	    && mv BLD-POTFILES-t BLD-POTFILES )

f=""; \
	for i in elf32-mips.lo elfxx-mips.lo elf-vxworks.lo elf32.lo elf.lo elflink.lo elf-attrs.lo elf-strtab.lo elf-eh-frame.lo dwarf1.lo ecofflink.lo coff-mips.lo ecoff.lo elfn32-mips.lo elf64-mips.lo elf64.lo elf64-gen.lo elf32-gen.lo cpu-mips.lo  archive64.lo ; do \
	  case " $f " in \
	    *" $i "*) ;; \
	    *) f="$f $i" ;; \
	  esac ; \
	done ; \
	echo $f > tofiles
/bin/bash ./../move-if-change tofiles ofiles
